## Image: 2014-12-14 17.40.02.jpg
**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is a grotesque, elderly male figure, carved from wood and painted in vibrant colors, presented in a diorama setting. He stands with legs slightly spread and knees bent, leaning forward, actively gripping the two wooden handles of a post-hole digger. His expression is exaggerated and toothy: a wide, open-mouthed grin reveals uneven, yellowed teeth (some missing) and a dark mouth interior. He has a large, bulbous red nose, deep-set dark eyes, prominent cheekbones, and extensive facial wrinkles and jowls, suggesting a weathered and somewhat manic disposition. A white cigarette or cigarillo, emitting a faint wisp of smoke, hangs from the corner of his mouth. He wears a dark, irregularly shaped cowboy hat with a wide brim and a crumpled crown. His attire includes a light tan long-sleeved shirt, a dark grey or black vest worn open, a red bandana with white polka dots tied around his neck, and light grey trousers with a distinct red patch on the left thigh. Dark brown or black boots complete his footwear. The post-hole digger has natural wood handles; the right handle is wrapped with rusty barbed wire. The metal digging head is dark grey with rust accents. The carving exhibits pronounced, angular facets throughout the figure and clothing, emphasizing the wood's texture. The diorama base features small gravel, larger stones, carved green cacti-like plants, whitish fungal growths, weathered wood pieces, and loose barbed wire coils. The background is a painted light blue sky with soft white clouds.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
Translating this character into a professional pencil sketch would emphasize the rough-hewn, angular nature of the carving. Strong, varied line weights would define the character's silhouette and the hard edges of carved planes. Heavy, confident outlines would delineate the hat, shoulders, and the tools, while slightly thinner but firm lines would render clothing folds and facial contours. Delicate, crisp lines would be used for details like individual teeth, the cigarette, the barbed wire, and the bandana's polka dots. Shading would be crucial for conveying depth and texture: deep cross-hatching or solid blacks would define shadows under the hat brim, within the mouth, and in deep wrinkles, enhancing the grotesque quality. Softer, blended shading would suggest rounded forms like the nose and cheeks. The distinct carved facets would be rendered with a combination of sharp lines and subtle tonal shifts, using darker values for recessed areas and lighter values for prominent edges. The material textures—rough wood, rusty metal, pebbled ground—would be indicated through varied pencil strokes, stippling, and precise hatching, all within a grayscale palette that faithfully translates the original color values into distinct tones.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**

*   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would show a forward-leaning, slightly hunched posture, dominated by the wide, crumpled brim of the cowboy hat. The head would be tilted slightly down, with the prominent, bulbous nose extending forward. The back of the figure would show a slight curvature. The left arm would be bent at the elbow, forearm angled downwards and forwards, clearly showing the hand gripping the left handle of the post-hole digger. The left leg would be bent at the knee, with the bulky boot resting flat. The post-hole digger's handle would extend downwards, its metal head resting on the ground near the boot, and the joint mechanism would be visible.

*   **Back View:** The wide, irregularly shaped back of the cowboy hat would be the most prominent feature, covering the head entirely. The back of the dark vest would cover the upper torso, with the lighter tan shirt visible beneath. Folds and creases would be evident in the carved shirt and vest, particularly across the shoulders and lower back. The red polka-dotted bandana would be visible around the neck, likely tied in a simple knot. The two wooden handles of the post-hole digger would be angled downwards, converging as they approach the ground, gripped by the hands. The slightly splayed, bent legs in the light grey trousers would be visible, showing more carved folds and seams.

*   **Right Side Profile:** Similar to the left profile, the silhouette would feature a forward-leaning stance with the expansive cowboy hat brim. The right side of the face would present the same exaggerated features, including the prominent nose and deep facial wrinkles, with the cigarette clearly visible in the corner of the mouth. The right arm, bent at the elbow, would show the hand firmly gripping the right handle of the post-hole digger. The distinctive rusty barbed wire wrapping around this handle would be a key visible detail. The right leg would be bent at the knee, with the sturdy boot on the ground. The post-hole digger's handle would extend downwards, its metal head resting on the ground.

Shading would be achieved through cross-hatching and stippling; deep, dark values would emphasize the shadows under the hat, within deep clothing creases, and beneath the character on the base. The distinctive faceted texture on the jacket and pants would be conveyed using angular planes of varying pencil tones to suggest carved surfaces, while smoother, softer shading would define the skin and the wooden chair. The back of the grey/silver jacket would confirm its tattered and torn nature, with the faceted carving texture prominent across the back and sleeves. The red polka-dotted bandana knot would be visible at the neck. The back of the brown shirt would show underneath the open jacket. The back of the character's head would be largely obscured by the hat. The simple wooden chair's back and rear legs would be fully visible, with subtle signs of wear. The slumped posture, with rounded shoulders, would be evident.
-   **Right Side Profile:** Similar to the left profile, the forward-slumped posture would dominate the silhouette. The hat brim would obscure the upper face. ## Image: 2014-12-14 17.40.32.jpg
**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**

The character is a jovial cowboy, astride a weary-looking mule, accompanied by a barking dog. The cowboy is carved with a wide-open, joyful grin, eyes squinted or closed in mirth, and shaggy blonde hair peeking from under a wide-brimmed white cowboy hat. A lit cigarette hangs from the right corner of his mouth. He is playing a light-colored acoustic guitar, with his right hand positioned for strumming and his left hand on the fretboard. He wears a light brown long-sleeved shirt with rolled-up cuffs, dark brown pants, and dark boots, with a spur visible on his left boot. A brown belt is around his waist, and a darker brown holster is strapped to his right hip. Visible carving textures define clothing folds and hair, with smoother finishes on skin. The mule has a brown coat with darker mane and tail, appears downtrodden with large, sad eyes, and long, flopped ears. It wears a brown saddle with a lighter blanket, a coiled lariat tied to the saddle, and brown and blue bridle/reins. A "CH" brand is visible on its left hindquarters. The dog is a small, black and tan/brown breed, its head thrown back in a howl or bark, with pointed ears and an uplifted tail. All figures are set on a reddish-brown "dirt" base with small rocks, featuring a two-post barbed wire fence to the left of the mule.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**

In a clean, highly polished black-and-white professional pencil character design sketch, this character would be rendered with a strong emphasis on varied line weight and subtle tonal gradation. Confident, firm lines would define the primary silhouettes of the cowboy, mule, and dog, establishing their forms. Thinner, more delicate lines would articulate internal details: the joyful creases around the cowboy's eyes and mouth, the texture of his blonde hair beneath the hat, the fabric folds of his shirt and pants, and the individual strands of the lariat. The wood carving's inherent texture would be translated into suggestive hatching or cross-hatching, particularly on the hat, hair, and saddle. Gradual pencil shading would create a sense of three-dimensionality, with smooth transitions from light to shadow. Deeper tones would indicate areas like the underside of the hat brim, the mule's mane and tail, the cowboy's boots, and the darker patches of the dog's fur, utilizing heavier graphite pressure. Highlights would be preserved as white or very light gray to suggest light reflection. The fence posts and barbed wire would be drawn with precise lines, and the ground texture indicated by subtle stippling or light shading, all devoid of color.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**

*   **Left Side Profile:** The cowboy's left profile would show his hat brim projecting forward, obscuring much of his forehead. His left arm would be bent, wrist angled to hold the guitar neck, fingers clearly detailed on the fretboard. His right arm would be largely concealed behind his torso and the guitar. His left leg, bent at the knee, would display the full length of his pant leg, boot, and the prominent spur, with the stirrup visible. The mule's full left profile would be clear, revealing its left eye, flopped left ear, and the distinctive "CH" brand on its hindquarters. Its left front leg would be raised in mid-stride. The dog's entire left profile would be visible, head tilted back, front left paw lifted, and tail curled upwards, engaged in its howl. The barbed wire fence would extend behind the mule's rear.

*   **Back View:** The cowboy's broad-brimmed white hat would dominate the upper back view, completely covering his hair and neck. The back of his light brown shirt would show natural, simple folds consistent with his slightly hunched guitar-playing posture, possibly with a subtle yoke across the shoulders. The back of his dark brown pants would be visible, creased, with stirrups and boots hanging below the mule's belly. The mule's rear would show its dark tail hanging down, possibly with a slight curve. The back of the saddle and the coiled lariat would be centered on the mule's spine. The dog would be seen from behind, positioned just to the mule's left rear, still with its head raised in a barking posture, its tail visible.

*   **Right Side Profile:** This view would mirror the left side profile for general proportions. The cowboy's hat brim would project forward. His right arm would be prominently displayed, bent at the elbow, hand actively strumming the guitar, with the elbow pointing slightly back. His left arm would be mostly obscured by the guitar and his torso. His right leg would be clearly visible, bent at the knee, with the boot and spur detailed. The mule's full right profile would be seen, showing its right eye and flopped right ear, without the "CH" brand. Its right front leg would be firmly on the ground, and its right rear leg slightly extended backward, suggesting movement. The dog's front-facing torso and head might be partially obscured by the mule's right front leg, or its back would be seen if it is positioned further out, still with its head raised. The barbed wire fence would be absent from this side.

## Image: 2014-12-14 17.40.55.jpg
Here is the character analysis:

**Character 1: The Dejected Cowboy (Slim)**

**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character stands with a slumped posture, weight shifted slightly to his right, left hand tucked deep into his front jeans pocket, and his right hand resting on his hip/back pocket. His head is tilted downwards and slightly left, conveying dejection. His expression features heavy eyelids, deeply carved wrinkles on his forehead and around his mouth, a drooping mustache, and a full beard. A lit cigarette dangles from his mouth. He wears a light brown, wide-brimmed cowboy hat, a faded light blue long-sleeved button-up shirt with rolled cuffs and an open collar revealing a darker brown undershirt. His baggy blue jeans are patched (one yellow/tan patch visible on the left thigh) and appear worn with tears. He wears brown, pointed-toe cowboy boots. The carving exhibits visible wood grain on the hat and boots, with rough, textured carving on the clothing to simulate fabric folds and wear. Facial features are deeply carved for strong shadow and expressive depth. All colors are muted and earthy with a matte paint finish.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
This character would feature strong, heavy outlines for his overall silhouette, hat, boots, and main body shape. Medium lines would define clothing seams, major fabric folds, and prominent facial features like eyes, nose, mouth, mustache, and beard. Finer, delicate lines would render subtle fabric textures, the cigarette, and stubble. Shading would primarily use cross-hatching and soft blending to indicate depth, with deep shadows under the hat brim, beneath the chin, and within clothing folds to translate the carving's dimensionality. Lighter shading would define the rounded forms of the hat and boots, and the contours of his face, with distinct textural shading for the patches and worn areas of his jeans. All color information would be conveyed through variations in tonal value and line density.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
*   **Left Side Profile:** His silhouette would appear hunched, with his head tilted forward. The hat brim would extend prominently forward and back. His left arm would be bent, hand deep in the front pocket, creating a distinct bulge. His right arm, angled slightly back, would have its hand in or near the back pocket, causing a subtle bend in the elbow and shoulder. The cigarette would protrude forward from his mouth.
*   **Back View:** The back of his wide-brimmed cowboy hat would be visible. His shoulders would appear slightly hunched. The back of his faded blue shirt would show vertical folds radiating from the upper back, indicating his slouch. Standard jeans back pockets would be visible, potentially with worn textures. His right hand would be partially seen, tucked into a back pocket or resting on the hip. His posture would be clearly slumped with a slightly bowed back, shifted to the right.
*   **Right Side Profile:** His silhouette would maintain the hunched posture. The hat brim would again be prominent. His right arm would be bent at the elbow, hand in the back pocket or resting on his hip, creating a slight indent or bulge in the clothing. His left arm would be angled slightly forward, hand in the front pocket, creating a noticeable bulge. The cigarette would appear as a small protrusion from his mouth.

**Character 2: The Matter-of-Fact Vendor**

**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character stands upright with a slightly puffed-out chest, his head turned slightly to his left, looking towards the cowboy. His expression is stern and matter-of-fact, characterized by wide-open eyes, raised eyebrows, an open mouth as if speaking, and visible forehead wrinkles. A subtle smirk is hinted. He wears a light-colored shirt with vertical dark stripes, a dark teal or black vest over it, with a gold watch chain draped across the front. He has dark, tailored trousers and polished dark shoes. A prominent yellow, oval-shaped belt buckle with red text ("FORT LEV... PENC") is visible. In his left hand, he holds an open brown cigar box with carved cigars inside, displaying "CIGARS 25¢" on its lid. His right hand is casually tucked into his pants pocket. The carving features smooth facial planes, emphasizing roundness, and crisp, defined lines for clothing folds, shirt stripes, and the vest. The belt buckle and watch chain have clear details and a slight sheen, while the overall paint finish is matte.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
This character would be rendered with strong, clean outlines for his overall figure, vest, shirt, trousers, and head. Medium lines would be used for the shirt stripes, vest seams, facial details (eyes, mouth, wrinkles), and the edges of the cigar box. Finer lines would define the watch chain, the belt buckle text, and the details of the carved cigars. Shading would utilize gradual, soft blending to depict the roundness of his head and stomach, complemented by cross-hatching for deeper shadows under the chin, within vest folds, and where the arm holds the cigar box. Shirt stripes would be represented by alternating bands of lighter and darker shading. The watch chain and belt buckle would incorporate subtle highlights and shading to convey a metallic texture. All color information would be translated into a range of tonal values and line variations.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
*   **Left Side Profile:** His silhouette would be upright and slightly portly, with his head tilted back slightly. His left arm would be bent at the elbow, holding the cigar box forward from his body at waist height. His right arm would be bent, hand in pocket, creating a slight bulge. The watch chain would be clearly visible, draped over the vest. The belt buckle would be visible as an oval shape.
*   **Back View:** The back of his dark vest would be prominent, likely with a smooth texture or subtle seam/cinch. The striped shirt would be visible underneath the vest, especially at the arms and collar. His dark trousers would show vertical folds or creases. His bald head would be visible from the top and back, showing any carved scalp texture or wrinkles. His posture would be upright and confident.
*   **Right Side Profile:** His silhouette would be upright and slightly portly. His right arm would be bent at the elbow, hand deep in his pants pocket, creating a noticeable bulge. His left arm, holding the cigar box, would be seen extending forward, with the back or side of the box clearly visible. The watch chain and belt buckle would be visible.

A matching pink and gold bridle with a scalloped chest strap adorns its head. Its mane and tail are white, textured with carved lines to simulate flowing hair. The hooves are black. The carving exhibits distinct facets and visible tool marks, indicating a hand-carved origin, with vibrant, opaque paint finishes that highlight the sculpted forms. The yellow mounting pole is fixed into a round, light wood base with a silver plaque reading "ONE MORE ROUND" and a carved signature "Coen."

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
Translated into a clean, highly polished black-and-white professional pencil character design sketch, this character would feature strong, consistent line weight defining the primary contours of the horse's body, saddle, pole, and base. Thinner, more delicate lines would delineate internal details such as the carved textures of the mane, tail, and furrowed brow, the straps of the bridle, the stitching on the saddle, the "CH" brand, and the details of the eyes. Shading would be achieved through smooth pencil gradients and precise cross-hatching, emphasizing the carved planes and roundness of the forms. Deep shadows would be present under the belly, beneath the saddle, and where the horse connects to the pole, adding depth. Highlights on the mane, tail, and sculpted surfaces would be rendered by leaving areas white or using minimal, light shading. The round base and pole would show gradient shading to convey their cylindrical form.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
-   **Left Side Profile:** The horse's silhouette is a dynamic, arched form. The front left leg is bent sharply upwards, tucked close to the body. The rear left leg is bent forward, hoof slightly off the ground. The mane flows backward from the arched neck, and the tail extends backward from the rump. The pink and turquoise saddle, complete with gold trim and carved stitching, clearly covers the back. The beige saddle blanket with the "CH" brand is prominent on the flank. The pink and gold bridle with its scalloped chest strap is fully visible on the head. The horse's blue eye and furrowed brow convey its wistful expression.
-   **Back View:** The central yellow pole would be prominently centered, extending vertically from the round wooden base to through the horse's body. The hindquarters of the horse form the main bulk, appearing rounded and powerful. The saddle's back edge, showing pink and turquoise, would wrap around the horse's back. The white, textured tail flows downward and slightly outward, covering much of the rear view. Parts of the inner/outer rear legs would be visible, positioned to indicate the galloping stride, with the hooves angled. The white mane would be visible draping over the neck, potentially parted slightly down the middle, with the top of the horse's head and ears visible above.
-   **Right Side Profile:** The silhouette largely mirrors the left side, depicting a dynamic, arched galloping horse. The unseen front right leg would be extended forward and slightly downward, as if reaching. The unseen rear right leg would be extended backward. The mane flows backward, and the tail extends from the rump. The pink and turquoise saddle with gold trim and carved stitching would cover the back, appearing as a mirror image of the left side. A beige saddle blanket would be present, but the "CH" brand would likely be absent from this flank, as brands are typically unilateral. The pink and gold bridle would adorn the head, a mirrored version of the left side's. The horse's right blue eye and furrowed brow would show the same wistful expression.

The character is an elderly, bearded male figure with a weary, downtrodden expression, featuring drooping eyelids and a downturned mouth, with a small white stub (cigarette or chewing tobacco) protruding from his lips. He is seated on a saddle atop a dark-colored horse or mule, leaning slightly forward, with both gloved hands gripping brown reins. He wears a light-colored, soft cap or bandana on his head, speckled with white dots, over a reddish-brown underlayer. His attire consists of a bulky, textured blue-grey jacket with lighter cream-colored trim around the collar, cuffs, and hem, and light yellow/ochre-colored, thick gloves or mittens. His pants are light off-white or cream, heavily textured with vertical folds, disappearing towards the horse's flank. A cylindrical yellow/ochre saddlebag is tied to the left side of the saddle, behind his leg. The animal is a sturdy, dark brown/black horse or mule with white "socks" on its lower legs and a white blaze/muzzle, displaying a sad, wide-eyed expression. It wears a simple brown bridle with a metal bit. The entire scene is set in snow, indicated by white carved ground texture and light dusting on a rustic split-rail fence and a wooden signpost. The signpost features two green directional signs pointing left: the top reads "NEW YORK!" and the bottom reads "TEXAS," both in white text. The carving exhibits visible tool marks, especially on clothing folds and the animal's fur, and the paint finish shows slight variations, suggesting hand-application and weathering.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
Translated into a black-and-white professional pencil sketch, the character would appear with clean, varied line weights: heavier lines defining the primary contours of the man, horse, signs, and fence, and thinner, more delicate lines for internal details. Facial features—drooping eyelids, downturned mouth, beard texture, and the stub—would be rendered with precise fine lines. Clothing folds on the jacket and pants, along with the textured trim, would be detailed with careful cross-hatching and parallel shading to convey depth, bulk, and material. The saddle, bridle straps, and saddlebag would have defined outlines and subtle shading to show their form and texture. The horse's musculature, mane, tail, and white markings would be depicted with smooth, darker shading for its body and lighter, textured shading for the white areas, emphasizing its weary expression. Snow on the ground and surfaces would be represented with minimal, light shading along edges for depth, contrasting with the dark outlines of footprints, and fine, sparse lines for dusted snow. The rustic wood grain on the fence and signpost, along with the "NEW YORK!" and "TEXAS" text, would be clearly delineated.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**

He has a droopy-eyed, slightly frowning expression with a prominent mustache and short beard. He wears a dark brown wide-brimmed hat, a rust-orange long-sleeved shirt, a dark brown vest with small light circular details, a light grey bandana with white polka dots around his neck, light tan trousers, and dark brown chaps/gaiters over clunky dark brown boots. A dark brown gun holster with a visible handgun is on his right hip, a coiled tan lasso hangs from the left side of his saddle, and a small dark brown bag hangs from the right side. The horse, facing left, also wears a sad, exaggerated expression with large, downturned eyes. Its body is primarily light brown with a dark brown mane, tail, and leg markings. A tan saddle with stirrups and a brown bridle are visible. The small, dark brown dog sits on its haunches to the right of the horse, looking up with an object (possibly a bone) in its mouth. The entire ensemble rests on a light brown, layered rock formation, detailed with visible chisel marks to simulate strata, and a small patch of lighter grit and a tiny green cactus on top. The base itself is a plain circular wooden block. The carving exhibits a rough, textured style with matte, muted paint finishes.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
Translated into a black-and-white professional pencil character design sketch, the cowboy, horse, and dog would be rendered with varied line weights: heavier for primary outlines to define forms and separation from the background, and lighter, finer lines for internal details. The cowboy's weary expression would be emphasized through detailed lines around the eyes and mouth, with textural lines for the mustache and beard. The rough, carved texture of the hat, clothing folds, and the horse's mane would be suggested through selective cross-hatching, stippling, and short, parallel lines. Shading would be applied to create depth and volume, mimicking the carved surfaces and implied shadows: darker gradients beneath the hat brim, within clothing folds (vest, bandana), and to define the horse's musculature and saddle contours. The layered texture of the rock formation would be conveyed with strong, defined contour lines and subtle shading to indicate depth and uneven surfaces. The dog's simple, rounded form would have lighter outlines and minimal shading. Highlights would be achieved by leaving areas pristine white, particularly on raised surfaces, to simulate light reflection on the carved wood, all without any color information.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
*   **Left Side Profile:** The cowboy's silhouette would show his broad shoulders and slightly hunched posture on the horse. His left arm would be bent at the elbow, hand holding the reins/resting on the saddle horn, while his right arm would be bent with the hand on his hip, the gun holster prominent behind it on the right hip. The coiled lasso would be clearly visible hanging from the left side of the saddle. The horse would be in full profile, its head still lowered, mane flowing down its neck, and its sad expression clearly visible. The dog would be in full profile, seated and looking up, with the object in its mouth visible. The layered rock base would be seen from the side, showcasing its stratified profile.
*   **Back View:** The cowboy's dark brown hat would be seen from the back, showing its crumpled texture and wide brim. The back of his rust-orange shirt and dark vest would be visible, with folds indicating his slightly slouched posture. The knot and ends of the bandana would be prominent at the back of his neck. His legs, encased in chaps/gaiters, would be visible from behind, obscuring the saddle somewhat. The horse's powerful hindquarters, muscular legs, and full, flowing dark brown tail would be central. The back of the saddle and saddle blanket would be visible. The small dog would be seen from behind, still seated and looking up, with the object in its mouth partially obscured by its head. The rock formation would wrap around, showcasing its textured, layered back surface.
*   **Right Side Profile:** The cowboy's silhouette would be similar to the left profile. His right arm would be bent with his hand on his hip, the gun holster with the visible handgun clearly featured on his right hip. His left arm would be resting on the saddle. The small dark brown bag would be visible hanging from the right side of the saddle. The coiled lasso would be partially visible from the far side (left) of the saddle, peeking out from behind the horse's body. The horse would be in full profile, head still lowered, with its sad expression and mane visible. The dog would be in full profile, seated and looking up, with the object in its mouth clearly visible. The layered rock base would be seen from the side, identical in profile to the left side, but with the cactus more prominent in the foreground.

POKE" in red, with its flag down and letters visible inside, is mounted on a wooden post connected by a copper-colored wire towards the cowboy's left. ## Image: 2014-12-19 12.46.58.png
**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is a caricatured baseball player with an exaggerated, grumpy expression. He stands slightly hunched, feet apart on a carved wooden base resembling a pitcher's mound. His prominent, ruddy nose and heavily furrowed brow give him a determined, somewhat stressed look, with small, deep-set eyes peering out. A scraggly dark beard and mustache cover his lower face, and his mouth is a tight, downward curve, occasionally revealing a few teeth in a sneer. He wears a dark baseball cap with a star emblem on the front, its brim pulled low. His uniform consists of an off-white, slightly baggy baseball jersey with dark grey trim on the sleeves and a large "1" on the back, paired with matching off-white pants tucked into dark grey/black cleats. His primary prop is a well-worn, dark brown baseball glove, held cupped in his right hand against his chest or side. The carving features a matte paint finish allowing subtle wood grain to show, with rougher texture for the beard and fine details like stitching on the glove. The base is natural wood, featuring a carved plaque that reads "THE LOOK" and the initials "GW."

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
This character translated into a black-and-white professional pencil sketch would use varied line weights to define its exaggerated forms. Thick, confident lines would establish the overall silhouette, the strong curve of the cap brim, and the main contours of the body and glove. Medium lines would delineate clothing folds, facial features like the prominent nose and deep brow lines, and the edges of the uniform trim. Fine, delicate lines would create texture for the scraggly beard and hair, the intricate lacing on the glove, and subtle creases in the uniform. Shading would be achieved through smooth graphite gradations for the roundness of limbs and face, while cross-hatching or stippling would render the beard, hair, and deeper shadows under the cap brim, within clothing folds, and around the glove. Strong contrast between highlights and shadows would emphasize the grumpy expression and solid form, with the number "1" on the back rendered as a solid, dark shape.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**

*   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would show a pronounced forward hunch, with the baseball cap brim extending significantly past the nose. The prominent nose would lead the facial profile, followed by the deep-set chin partially obscured by the beard. The uniform would show a slight bulge for the belly. The left arm would be bent at the elbow, hand resting near the hip, while the right arm would be bent, holding the baseball glove tightly against the chest, showcasing the glove's thick, cupped profile and thumb area extending forward. The left leg would appear straighter, the right leg bent back.
*   **Back View:** The uniform would be the central focus, displaying the number "1" clearly on the back of the jersey. Natural folds and creases would be visible across the shoulders, down the back, and around the waistline where the jersey tucks into the pants. The back of the baseball cap would show its rounded form and potentially a seam. The scraggly hair and beard would extend from beneath the cap, framing the neck. The legs would be seen extending down to the dark cleats, with the slight separation of the feet visible.
*   **Right Side Profile:** Similar to the left profile, but with the body's weight distribution and arm positions mirrored. The silhouette would maintain the forward hunch and prominent cap brim. The facial profile would show the back of the ear (partially obscured by hair/beard), a prominent cheekbone, and the back of the nose. The right arm would be bent, with the back of the hand visible gripping the baseball glove, which would be seen from its palm/back side against the torso, showing texture and the wrist opening. The left arm would be bent, hand near the hip, mostly obscured by the body. The right leg would be slightly forward, and the left leg bent back.

## Image: 2014-12-19 12.49.34.png
**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is an exaggerated, caricatured baseball pitcher mid-pitch or pre-pitch. He is posed in a deep, forward lean with his back hunched, legs bent, and feet planted. His right arm is cocked back holding a white baseball, while his left arm is bent at the elbow, and his gloved hand rests near his left knee or lower thigh. His head is titled down and forward, wearing a black baseball cap with a white "CH" or "H" logo. His expression is intense and focused, with squinted eyes, a prominent large nose, and a thick, textured beard covering his jawline and chin. His mouth appears slightly open or a dark void. He wears an off-white/cream baseball jersey with black sleeves and visible black number "7" on the right sleeve. His left hand wears a brown baseball glove. He stands on a carved, earthy mound atop a circular wooden base. The carving features rough, faceted textures, particularly noticeable on the uniform folds, beard, and cap. The uniform, skin, and cap have a matte paint finish, while the baseballs appear glossy. The wooden base varies from dark walnut to lighter oak, some featuring a carved plaque stating "THE SIGN" with a stylized 'S', and others including "EH '19" carved into the wood.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
Translated into a black-and-white pencil sketch, the character would maintain its exaggerated proportions and dynamic pose. Line weight would vary: thick, bold lines would define the character's silhouette, the brim of the cap, the glove, and the edges of major forms. Thinner lines would render internal details like beard texture, uniform seams, fabric creases, and the stitching on the baseball. Shading would be achieved through careful cross-hatching and parallel lines, mimicking the faceted texture of the wood carving. Deeper recesses, such as under the cap brim, within the folds of the uniform, and inside the glove, would receive darker, denser shading. Highlights would be depicted by leaving areas of the paper white or using very light tonal values on prominent planes. Cast shadows from the cap onto the face, and from arms/torso onto the uniform, would add depth and volume.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
-   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would show a prominent hunched back, the large cap, and the exaggerated nose. The left arm, encased in the brown baseball glove, would be bent, with the glove clearly visible and facing slightly forward or inward towards the body. The right arm, holding the baseball, would extend distinctly backward, bent at the elbow, with the baseball visible from the side as a circular form at the end of the extended hand. The thick beard would be visible, wrapping around the jawline. The exaggerated gut due to the forward lean would be apparent.
-   **Back View:** The character's back would be heavily rounded and hunched from the deep forward lean. The back of the baseball cap would be a smooth, dark curve covering the head. The cream jersey would show significant horizontal and diagonal folds across the back due to the compressed posture. The shoulders would appear broad, possibly slightly offset from the body's twist. No numbers or specific details would likely be visible on the plain back of the jersey. The bent legs would be clearly visible, with the cleats planted.
-   **Right Side Profile:** The silhouette would mirror the hunched, leaning posture. The right arm would be fully extended backward, bent at the elbow, with the baseball prominently held and clearly visible from this angle. The left arm, with its glove, would be largely obscured by the character's torso and the extended right arm, possibly only showing a hint of the glove's edge or upper arm. The face, including the large nose, thick beard, and cap, would be clearly visible and angled downward, maintaining the intense expression.

## Image: 2014-12-19 13.03.47.png
**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is a male baseball pitcher, highly caricatured, with an exaggerated head and facial features. He is captured in a dynamic pitching pose, leaning forward and twisting his torso to the left (his left). His left leg is bent at the knee and planted on a carved wooden mound base, while his right leg is extended backward, heel lifted. His left arm is fully extended forward and slightly down, hand open, holding a carved baseball. His right arm is bent at the elbow, with a brown catcher's mitt on his hand, pulled back close to his body. His head is turned to his left, eyes focused intensely in the direction of the throw, featuring a large, broad nose, bushy brown beard and mustache, furrowed brows, and an open mouth with a hint of tongue. He wears a light cream/off-white baseball uniform with black trim on the sleeves and collar, a black number "1" on the chest, matching pants with black piping, black baseball cleats, and a dark grey/black baseball cap with a white "H" logo. The entire carving exhibits a hand-carved, somewhat rustic texture, particularly visible in the wood grain of the base, the folds of the uniform, and the carved strands of hair and beard. The uniform is painted, while the skin appears to be natural wood. A signature, "C. Gray" (or similar), is carved into the side of the main figure's wooden mound, and a small plaque on the larger base in the bottom right image reads "THE STRETCH."

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
Translated to a black-and-white professional pencil character design sketch, this character would maintain his exaggerated proportions and dynamic pitching pose. Primary outlines, such as the overall silhouette of the figure, the cap, the limbs, and the base, would be rendered with strong, confident line weights. Internal details like facial features (nose, eyes, mouth, beard outline), major uniform folds, the baseball, and the mitt would use medium line weights. Finer, lighter lines would define subtle textures like individual strands of hair and beard, stitching on the baseball, uniform seams, and the carved wood grain of the base. Shading would be achieved through soft pencil tones and controlled cross-hatching, creating depth and volume. Darker shading would be concentrated in areas of shadow, such as under the cap brim, beneath the chin, deep within the uniform folds, the underside of the limbs, inside the mitt, and recessed areas of the base. Lighter shading would highlight the contours of the cap, shoulders, chest, and arms, defining the character's three-dimensional form without color.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**

*   **Left Side Profile:**
    *   **Silhouette:** The silhouette would be lean and dynamic. The cap's brim would extend forward, partially obscuring the top of the face. The prominent nose and beard would jut out. The long, messy hair would be visible extending from under the back of the cap. The left arm would be fully extended forward and slightly downwards, holding the baseball. The torso would appear twisted towards the viewer. The right arm, holding the mitt, would be mostly obscured behind the torso, with perhaps only the elbow or a hint of the mitt visible behind the body's center line. The left leg would be sharply bent at the knee, foot planted on the circular base. The right leg would extend backward, revealing the bent knee and the cleated foot trailing behind.
    *   **Arm setup:** Left arm fully extended forward, straight or slightly bent, hand open and grasping the baseball. Right arm bent, mostly hidden behind the body, mitt facing rearward or downward.
    *   **Props:** The baseball held in the left hand would be clearly visible. The catcher's mitt on the right hand would be largely obscured by the character's torso and arm from this angle.

*   **Back View:**
    *   **Back of clothing:** The back of the cream/off-white jersey would display pronounced folds and wrinkles from the torso's dynamic twisting. The black trim on the short sleeves would be visible. The number "1" on the chest would not be present. The back of the pants would show the strong bend at the left knee and the full extension of the right leg, with both black cleats distinctly visible.
    *   **Hat/Hair:** The back of the black baseball cap would be visible, likely plain without a logo. The long, messy brown hair, carved with distinct strands, would cascade from under the cap.
    *   **Posture:** The extreme twist of the torso and shoulders would be evident, showing the dynamic motion. The left arm would be extended away from the body, while the right arm, with the mitt, would be bent and pulled inward towards the right side of the back. The full leg extension and bend would be clearly defined.

*   **Right Side Profile:**
    *   **Silhouette:** A dynamic, mirrored silhouette compared to the left side. The cap brim would still extend forward, covering the upper face. The large nose and bushy beard would remain prominent. The messy hair would be visible flowing from the back of the cap. The right arm, bent at the elbow, would be prominently displayed with the catcher's mitt facing forward or slightly upward. The left arm, holding the baseball, would be extended forward but mostly obscured behind the torso or visible reaching out from behind. The right leg would be extended backward. The left leg would be bent forward, with the foot planted on the mound base.
    *   **Arm setup:** Right arm bent at the elbow, pulled back, with the catcher's mitt clearly displayed. Left arm extended forward, largely obscured by the torso, with the baseball potentially peeking out or visible further in the distance.
    *   **Props:** The catcher's mitt would be the dominant prop on this side, prominently visible on the right hand. The baseball in the left hand would be mostly obscured by the torso, or appear further away in the background.

## Image: 2014-12-19 13.03.55.png
**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is a male caricature-style baseball pitcher. He is captured in a dynamic mid-pitch pose, leaning forward with his right arm fully extended, releasing the baseball. His left arm is bent, holding a tan baseball mitt close to his chest. His right leg is extended backward, and his left leg is bent forward. He wears a dark grey baseball cap with a white "CH" logo, a cream-colored uniform top with black sleeves and piping (showing a "1" on the back), cream pants with black side stripes, and black cleats. His face displays an intense, focused expression with a slightly open mouth, prominent nose, bushy eyebrows, and a textured beard/sideburns. The baseball in his right hand has red stitching. Visible carving textures are rough and chiseled on hair, beard, uniform creases, and the mitt, contrasting with natural wood tones for skin and a smooth-sanded base.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
This character would translate as a highly expressive, dynamic figure in black-and-white pencil. Line weight would be varied: thick outlines for the overall silhouette, limbs, and base, with finer lines defining internal details like uniform seams, facial contours, individual hair strands, glove stitching, and baseball seams. Shading would utilize soft, blended pencil tones to convey volumetric form, especially on the face, roundness of the cap, and muscular tension in the uniform. Cross-hatching could suggest fabric texture and deeper shadows. The "CH" logo, uniform "1", sleeves, and stripes would be rendered as solid dark areas, while the cream parts of the uniform would be lighter grey tones, all without color.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**

*   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would show the prominent forward lean of the torso and head. The right arm would extend directly forward, appearing as a straight line from shoulder to hand, with the perfectly round baseball at its end. The bent left arm would hold the glove, showing its full profile against the chest. The left leg would be planted forward, bent at the knee, with the right leg trailing back. The cap's brim would clearly project forward.

*   **Back View:** The uniform top would clearly display the dark number "1" centered on the back. Deep creases would radiate from the shoulder blades and lower back, emphasizing the torso's twisting motion. The back of the baseball cap would cover the head, with some textured hair likely visible from underneath at the nape of the neck. The right leg would be fully extended backward and possibly angled upward, revealing the calf and heel, while the left leg would be bent with its heel lifted.

*   **Right Side Profile:** The silhouette would mirror the forward lean of the left profile. The right arm would extend directly forward, but the inner elbow and arm would be visible leading to the hand holding the baseball. The left arm and glove would be largely obscured by the torso and the extended right arm. The right leg would be extended backward and upward, revealing the inner side of the thigh and foot. The left leg would be planted forward.

**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is a male baseball pitcher in a dynamic windup pose. He stands on his right leg, which is planted on a stylized wooden mound, with his left leg raised high and bent at the knee. His torso is twisted to his left, leaning slightly forward. His facial expression is a grimace of intense effort, with wide-set eyes, a prominent upturned nose, and a bushy brown beard that merges into sideburns. He wears a white baseball uniform with black trim/piping, visible number "1" on his back, and a dark grey or black baseball cap featuring a stylized white "H" logo on the front. His left hand, covered by a black catcher's glove, is extended forward, while his right hand holds a light brown baseball, drawn back as if preparing to throw. The carving exhibits visible facets and textures, particularly on the hair, beard, cap, and the base, with a matte painted finish on the uniform and skin tones.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
Translated into a professional pencil sketch, the character would feature crisp, varied line weights to define his form. Outlines would be strong and confident, emphasizing the exaggerated silhouette and dynamic pose. Internal lines would define the sharp angles and planes of the wood carving, especially on the face, beard, and cap. Shading would be achieved through cross-hatching and soft pencil rendering, creating deep shadows under the brim of the cap, within the folds of the uniform, and on the textured beard and glove. Highlights would be minimal, suggested by unshaded areas or lighter lines, to convey volume and depth without color. The facial grimace and intense gaze would be accentuated by heavier lines around the eyes and mouth.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
-   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would show a dramatically forward-leaning torso and a high, acutely bent left leg. The right leg would be firmly planted, with a clear view of the foot on the mound. The left arm, with the black glove, would be fully extended forward. The right arm, holding the baseball, would be bent and drawn back, its elbow high and visible. The prominent nose and full beard would be clearly silhouetted against the face, with the cap brim extending forward.
-   **Back View:** The uniform's back would show prominent folds and wrinkles, conforming to the twisted torso. The number "1" would be centered and clearly visible on the back. Black piping would outline the sleeves and back seams. The back of the dark cap would cover the head, with the bushy brown hair/beard extending from beneath it, obscuring the neck. The raised left leg would be seen from behind, bent at the knee, with the right leg planted firmly.
-   **Right Side Profile:** The silhouette would mirror the left profile in terms of leg and torso positioning, showcasing the dynamic forward lean and high raised left leg. The right arm, holding the baseball, would be prominently featured, drawn back with the elbow high. The left arm, with the glove, would be extended forward but partially obscured by the torso. The profile of the cap, beard, and facial grimace would be visible, but the prominent nose would be less emphasized than from the left side.

## Image: 2015-01-02 13.50.21.jpg
**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is an aged man, reminiscent of Moses, with a weary expression, furrowed brow, and slightly open mouth. He stands with a slight slouch, his head tilted upwards and to his left. He has a long, voluminous, greyish-brown beard and wavy hair that flows down to his chest and shoulders. His skin is a reddish-brown tone. He wears a loose, off-white or light-colored robe with purple trim on the cuffs and possibly the collar. His feet are bare with visible toes, wearing brown sandals. In his right hand (viewer's left), he holds a long, gnarled brown wooden staff that leans against his shoulder. In his left hand (viewer's right), he holds a brown water skin or jug with a small red label, resting against his hip. Behind him is a dark wooden signpost with two diverging arrows: one pointing left, labeled "PROMISED LAND" on a blue sign, and another pointing right, labeled "MARGARITAVILLE" on a green sign. He stands on a round, light brown carved wooden base with prominent tool marks. A scroll-like banner is affixed to the front of the base, reading "MOSES' DILEMMA" in black text. The entire piece shows visible wood grain and textured carving, particularly on the hair, beard, staff, and base, with painted details.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
The character would be rendered with varied line weights; thicker lines defining the overall silhouette of the figure, base, and signpost, and thinner, more delicate lines for internal details like facial wrinkles, individual strands of hair and beard, folds in the robe, and the carved texture of the staff and base. Cross-hatching and stippling would be used to indicate the depth and texture of the wood carving, especially on the beard, hair, and base, while smoother gradients would define the form of the robe and body. Shadows would be clearly defined to give a three-dimensional effect, indicating the carved depressions and protrusions. The text on the signs and banner would be clear and legible. No color would be used, relying solely on line and tone.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
-   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would show his slightly hunched posture. His long, wavy hair and beard would flow down the left side of his face and body. The right arm, holding the staff, would be seen extending down and slightly backward, with the full length and gnarled texture of the staff clearly visible from his hand to the base. His left arm, holding the water skin, would be pressed against his torso, with the water skin visible in profile. The "PROMISED LAND" sign would be partially visible behind his head, while the "MARGARITAVILLE" sign would be mostly obscured. The simple, flowing side of his robe and his sandal-clad foot would complete the profile on the round base.
-   **Back View:** The long, thick, wavy greyish-brown hair would cascade down his back, covering his shoulders. The back of his loose-fitting robe would show simple vertical folds, with the purple trim visible on the back of the sleeves. The staff would be seen extending downwards along his right side, and the water skin would be visible against his left hip. The wooden signpost, with both the "PROMISED LAND" (blue) and "MARGARITAVILLE" (green) signs, would be prominently displayed behind him, slightly off-center, anchored to the round, textured wooden base.
-   **Right Side Profile:** Similar to the left profile, showing his slightly hunched posture. His long, wavy hair and beard would flow down the right side of his face and body. The left arm, holding the water skin, would be seen extended down and slightly backward, with the full form of the water skin clearly visible from his hand to just above the base. His right arm, holding the staff, would be pressed against his torso, with the staff handle visible in profile. The "MARGARITAVILLE" sign would be partially visible behind his head, while the "PROMISED LAND" sign would be mostly obscured. The simple, flowing side of his robe and his sandal-clad foot would complete the profile on the round base.

## Image: 2015-01-02 13.51.48.jpg
**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is a wood-carved figure of an elderly man, likely Moses, standing on a round, multi-tiered wooden base. He stands slightly hunched forward, his head tilted slightly to the right with an upward gaze. His expression is contemplative and slightly exasperated, with furrowed brows and a slightly agape mouth framed by a long, textured white beard and mustache. He wears small, round dark spectacles. He is clad in a flowing, floor-length white robe with sculpted folds and creases. His feet wear brown sandals with purple straps. He holds a gnarled wooden staff in his right hand, its top curving backward. His left hand is raised near his face, holding a small, rectangular, dark gray object resembling a smartphone, from which a wavy "thought bubble" line emerges. At his feet, resting on the base, are two bound, rectangular stone tablets with a purple strap. Behind him, a wooden signpost features two directional arrows: one pointing left, labeled "PROMISED LAND" in blue-green, and one pointing right, labeled "MARGARITAVILLE" in blue-green. A carved banner reading "MOSES' DILEMMA" is attached to the front of the base. The carving exhibits visible tool marks and a rustic, earthy painted finish, with natural wood tones, muted white, purple, and blue-green accents.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
This character would translate into a black-and-white sketch with distinct line weights and nuanced shading. Primary forms like the figure's silhouette, major garment folds, staff, and base would be defined by confident, varying line weights, with heavier lines used for undersides and shadows to convey depth. Fine, delicate lines would render the individual strands of the beard and hair, the facial wrinkles, spectacle frames, sandal straps, and the text on the signs and base banner. Shading would be achieved through cross-hatching, stippling, and smooth tonal gradients. Deep shadows would be rendered with dense hatching in garment folds and beneath the beard, while lighter, smoother shading would define the wood texture of the staff and base, and the volume of the figure. The "thought bubble" line would be a thin, wavy line. The overall sketch would emphasize the carved textures and three-dimensionality of the original piece, using tonal contrast to differentiate materials and light.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
*   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would prominently feature his aquiline nose, the full, forward-flowing beard, and his hunched posture. His left arm would be clearly visible, bent at the elbow, hand holding the "smartphone" which would be seen from its side view, revealing its thickness. The staff held in his right hand would be mostly obscured by his body, appearing just behind his arm. The flowing white robe would drape backward, showing its volume. The "PROMISED LAND" sign would be seen in profile behind him, revealing its thickness and attachment to the post. The Ten Commandments tablets would be seen from their side, resting against the base.
*   **Back View:** The back of the flowing white robe would be the dominant feature, with vertical folds cascading down from the shoulders and lower back, emphasizing the fabric's drape. His long, shaggy hair would be visible, covering the back of his head and neck, consistent with the texture of his beard. No hat would be present. His posture would show a slight forward hunch. The vertical signpost would be centered behind him, showing the plain backs of both the "PROMISED LAND" and "MARGARITAVILLE" signs. The staff would extend down his right side, partially obscured by his robe.
*   **Right Side Profile:** The silhouette would show his right facial profile, with the beard extending downward. His right arm would be distinctly visible, bent at the elbow, firmly grasping the top of the staff. The staff would extend downwards, revealing its gnarled texture and slight backward angle. His left arm, holding the "smartphone," would be largely obscured by his body and beard, perhaps with just the device peeking out. The flowing white robe would form the main body silhouette. The "MARGARITAVILLE" sign would be visible in profile behind him, revealing its thickness and attachment to the post. The Ten Commandments tablets would be seen from their side, resting against the base.

**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is an elderly man, likely Moses, carved from wood with a folk art aesthetic. He stands slightly hunched, looking upward and to his left. His expression is thoughtful, with a large nose, rosy cheeks, and a very long, full white beard that covers his mouth. He wears a simple, light-colored, long-sleeved robe and open-toed sandals. A small brown head covering rests on his head. He holds a rustic wooden staff in his right hand. In his left hand, he holds a dark pipe with a small grey smoke puff rising from it, while also giving a thumbs-up gesture. At his feet, a maroon satchel labeled "MILK AND HONEY OR BUST" rests. Behind him is a rough-hewn wooden signpost with two green directional signs: "PROMISED LAND" pointing left, and "MARGARITAVILLE" pointing right. The carving displays visible wood grain and textured finishes, particularly in the beard, robe folds, and weathered signs. The base is a stack of carved wooden discs, with a small brown plaque on the lower disc reading "MOSES DAY".

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
This character, translated into a black-and-white professional pencil sketch, would feature strong, varied line weights. Outlines of the figure, staff, signpost, and base would use thicker, confident lines to define their forms. Internal details like the beard strands, facial wrinkles, robe folds, and sandal straps would be rendered with finer, precise lines. Shading would be achieved through soft pencil gradients for general volume and texture, complemented by cross-hatching and hatching to indicate deeper shadows (e.g., under the beard, within robe folds, under the pipe and smoke, on the undersides of the signs) and to suggest the wood grain texture of the staff and signpost. The "MILK AND HONEY OR BUST" and "MOSES DAY" text would be clearly legible, outlined and filled without color.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
-   **Left Side Profile:** The character's silhouette would show a slight forward lean and the full drape of the robe, possibly with a subtle outward curve at the lower back from the posture. The profile of his face, prominent nose, and the long, flowing beard would be clearly visible. The right arm, holding the staff, would extend downwards, with the staff visible from end to end. The left arm would be bent, likely mostly obscured by the body, with possibly the pipe and thumbs-up hand peeking out. The suitcase would be clearly visible on the ground. The signpost behind him would show its thickness.
-   **Back View:** The back of the character would show the simple, flowing drape of his robe, with vertical folds indicating fabric movement. The back of the head covering would be visible, with the long, full beard extending downward from his head, possibly parting slightly at the bottom. The staff would be seen held by his right hand, extending vertically. His left arm would be mostly hidden by his body. The full back of the signpost and the two green directional signs would be prominently displayed. The suitcase might be partially visible behind his lower legs.
-   **Right Side Profile:** The character's silhouette would mirror the left profile, showing the full robe and slight forward lean. The profile of his face, large nose, and beard would be visible, with perhaps a glimpse of his left eye. His left arm would be prominently bent at the elbow, clearly showing the pipe held by his hand and the distinct thumbs-up gesture, with the smoke puff visible above the pipe. The right arm and staff would be largely obscured by his body. The suitcase would be clearly visible at his feet, facing the viewer with its label. The signpost would be visible from the side, showcasing its thickness.

**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
The character is a stout, unpainted wood carving of a male figure with a grumpy, determined expression, lying horizontally on a wooden surface. He wears a wide-brimmed cowboy hat, deeply furrowed brow, prominent nose, and a scowling mouth. His clothing includes a button-down shirt with carved folds suggesting a placket and collar, a belt line, and thick pants that lead into large, rounded boots. His arms are bent at the elbow, and his hands are sculpted into thick, somewhat clenched fists. The entire carving is a natural light wood color, displaying visible facets and tool marks from the carving process, indicating an unfinished or rustic aesthetic.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
In a clean, highly polished black-and-white professional pencil character design sketch, the character would be rendered with a strong interplay of varied line weights. Heavier, crisp lines would define the primary contours of the hat, head, torso, limbs, and boots, giving the figure a solid, grounded presence. Lighter, more delicate lines, possibly with fine cross-hatching or smooth gradient shading, would delineate the internal details such as facial features (furrows, nose creases, mouth lines), clothing folds, the texture of the hat, and the distinct facets and planes of the original carving. Shading would be used to create deep shadows under the hat brim and within clothing folds, emphasizing the character's volume and the rugged texture of his attire, while completely omitting color.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
-   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would show the distinct curve of the hat brim and crown extending forward and slightly upward. The head would appear pushed forward, with a prominent nose and chin. The chest would be broad, leading to a noticeable belly and a sturdy back. The left arm would be bent, likely with the hand resting on the hip or side of the thigh. The thick pant leg would curve into a robust, chunky boot with a defined sole.
-   **Back View:** The back of the wide-brimmed cowboy hat would dominate the top, showing the curve of the crown and brim. Below the hat, the back of the shirt would feature a prominent collar, possibly a yoke, and vertical folds indicating movement or thickness. A defined belt line would encircle the waist. The back of the pants would show creasing, and the sturdy, rounded backs of the boots would complete the figure. No hair would be visible beneath the hat. The posture would be slightly hunched but solid.
-   **Right Side Profile:** This view would largely mirror the Left Side Profile, showcasing the same sturdy silhouette, hat shape, and robust physique. The right arm would be bent at the elbow, with the hand positioned similarly to the left, likely on the hip or resting on the side. The facial features would be visible from this angle, showing the forward-tilting head, strong nose, and determined chin. The thick pant leg would flow into the solid, rounded boot.

His left arm is extended forward and slightly downwards, holding a thin, curved, dark brown riding crop or stick. He is seated on and appears to be operating a simple, three-wheeled wooden tricycle. The carving exhibits distinct, clean facets across the figure, hat, and beard, highlighting the carving process, while the tricycle's wheels are smooth and spoked. The entire piece is rendered in the natural, unpainted light tone of the wood, with the exception of the dark brown riding crop.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
In a black-and-white pencil sketch, this character would feature strong, varied line weights: thick, confident lines would define the primary silhouette of the figure, hat, and tricycle, emphasizing their overall form. Thinner, precise lines would delineate facial features, beard strands, clothing folds, and the details of the mug and riding crop. Shading would be achieved through controlled cross-hatching and stippling to represent the carved facets and wood texture, particularly on the figure and beard. Smoother, graduated shading would be applied to the wheels and mug to convey their roundness. Deep, dark shading would be utilized in recesses such as under the hat brim, within the beard's depth, and beneath limbs to create strong contrast and volume. The dark riding crop would be rendered with a denser, almost charcoal-like tone to distinguish its material and color.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
-   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would show the character leaning forward. His left arm would be fully extended forward and slightly down, holding the riding crop with its curve pointing towards the ground. His right arm, holding the mug, would be bent sharply at the elbow, with the mug partially visible against his torso. The tall top hat would be prominent, tilted forward. The flowing beard would sweep back from his chin. His left leg would be clearly visible, bent at the knee and extended forward, with the right leg positioned slightly further back. The tricycle's single front wheel and two rear wheels would form a clear profile of its frame.
-   **Back View:** The back of the tall, cylindrical top hat with its flat brim would dominate the upper portion. Below it, the back of his head and neck would be visible. His coat or jacket would likely feature a simple, unadorned back, possibly with subtle indications of a center seam or pleats, and without dramatic tails based on the front view. His broad shoulders and upper back would be clear, with his arms angled outwards and downwards, reflecting their forward pose. The back of his bent legs would be visible, positioned over the tricycle's simple wooden seat. The rear of the tricycle's frame, including the two spoked rear wheels and the axle, would be the most prominent feature of the vehicle.
-   **Right Side Profile:** The silhouette would again show the character leaning forward. His right arm would be bent at the elbow, holding the cylindrical mug prominently against his side. His left arm, fully extended, would show the shaft of the dark riding crop extending forward from his hand, with the curved tip visible near the ground. The top hat would be tilted forward. The beard would be visible, framing the side of his face. His right leg would be extended forward and bent, while his left leg would be positioned slightly further back. The tricycle's wheels and frame would present a clear profile, with the single front wheel and two rear wheels indicating its structure.

The left arm would be partially obscured by the torso, appearing as a slight curve behind the body. The book would be clearly visible, held against the chest.

## Image: 2015-05-14 16.01.10.jpg
**1. COLOR WOOD CARVING PORTRAIT**
This is an unfinished, light-toned wood carving of a jovial male character, likely a gnome or old man. He stands upright on a thick, irregular oval base. His body is slightly turned to his left, with a gentle forward lean. His left arm is bent, and his left hand cups the rolled brim of his pointed cap near his temple. His right arm is bent at the elbow, and his right hand rests on his lower stomach area, partially obscured by his left arm. He sports a wide, beaming smile, with deeply carved lines extending from his nose to his raised, full cheeks, and crows' feet around his closed or squinting eyes, conveying a cheerful demeanor. He wears a tall, pointed cap with a rolled brim, a long-sleeved top or tunic with visible fabric folds and wrinkles, and full pants tucked into sturdy, rounded boots with defined toes. The entire piece is carved from uniform, light-colored wood, exhibiting no paint or stain. Surfaces are smoothed but retain distinct, rounded facets and contours from hand carving, with subtle tool marks visible, especially on the base.

**2. SKETCH TRANSLATION**
Translated into a clean, highly polished black-and-white professional pencil character design sketch, this character would feature varied line weights. Thicker, darker lines would define the character's overall silhouette, major clothing folds, the prominent smile lines, and the hat brim. Thinner, lighter lines would delineate subtle details like minor wrinkles in clothing, finger definitions on the hat, and internal facial contours. Smooth graphite shading would render the character's volumetric form, implying a consistent light source (e.g., top-left). Shadows would fall under the hat brim, beneath the nose, within deep clothing folds, and where limbs overlap the torso, providing depth. Mid-tones would define the rounded surfaces of the face, limbs, and clothing. Subtle highlights would appear on the most exposed, rounded surfaces like the forehead, nose tip, and boot tops, using minimal graphite. The raw wood texture would be subtly suggested through very fine, tight cross-hatching or stippling in mid-tone areas.

**3. 4-SIDED TURNAROUND PREDICTION**
-   **Left Side Profile:** The silhouette would show the sharp peak of the pointed hat. The head would be slightly tilted forward. The left arm would be sharply bent at the elbow, with the forearm extending slightly forward, hand cupping the hat brim at the temple. The right arm would hang mostly straight down, close to the body, largely obscured by the torso. The body would show a slight forward lean, with a rounded stomach and a straighter back. Both legs and sturdy, forward-leaning boots would be clearly visible. The thick, irregular oval base would be prominent.
-   **Back View:** The back of the pointed hat would rise to its conical peak, potentially showing a slight curl. The tunic or shirt would drape cleanly, with vertical folds emanating from the shoulders and a central back seam or fold. A subtle belt line might be visible across the lower back. The fabric would fall over rounded buttocks. The full pant legs would meet the robust, rounded heels of the boots. No hair would be visible beneath the hat. The overall posture would appear slightly hunched forward from the shoulders.
-   **Right Side Profile:** The silhouette would again feature the pointed hat peak. The face would be less visible, showing the rounded cheek and jawline. The chest would be slightly prominent, flowing into the stomach and back. The left arm would be largely obscured by the torso, with only a potential glimpse of the elbow or forearm extending behind. The right arm would be more visible, bent at the elbow, with the forearm angled slightly forward, and the hand resting relaxed against the lower torso or stomach area. Both legs and sturdy, forward-leaning boots would be clearly visible. The thick, irregular oval base would be prominent.
